    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_36031167" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/36031167" />
    <a title="Trudi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1416912-trudi"><img alt="Trudi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1446613110p2/1416912.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/36031167?book_show_action=true">Oct 23, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1416912-trudi?shelf=non-fiction">non-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1416912-trudi?shelf=crime-mystery">crime-mystery</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer36031167" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8577513544691416491">I don't think you can <a href='http://www.imdb.com/title/tt0443706/' rel='nofollow noopener'>watch the film adaptation</a> and remain unmoved by Graysmith's story and his obsessive quest to uncover the identity of the Zodiac killer. There was no question that I had to read his book. Graysmith was a cartoonist by occupation, not a journalist, and it shows. He makes the number one blunder of any amateur writer of either fiction or non-fiction -- he tries to include <i>every last detail</i>. Graysmith's obsession with the Zodiac killer means every minutiae of the case is deemed </span>
  <span id="freeText8577513544691416491" style="display:none">I don't think you can <a href="http://www.imdb.com/title/tt0443706/" rel="nofollow noopener">watch the film adaptation</a> and remain unmoved by Graysmith's story and his obsessive quest to uncover the identity of the Zodiac killer. There was no question that I had to read his book. Graysmith was a cartoonist by occupation, not a journalist, and it shows. He makes the number one blunder of any amateur writer of either fiction or non-fiction -- he tries to include <i>every last detail</i>. Graysmith's obsession with the Zodiac killer means every minutiae of the case is deemed critical. As a reader, you're completely snowballed by facts and circumstances. I'm not a fan of police procedurals anyway, so this proved to be a bit much for me. <a href="http://www.imdb.com/title/tt0443706/" rel="nofollow noopener">Watch the movie</a>; it's quite excellent.</span>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer374632132" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3148949213457348115">What i really like about this book was how it was told and how it was layed out.<br/>Mr. Graysmith was a Newspaper cartoonist who later became involved in the Zodiac case. Not by his volition but, by the Zodiacs.<br/><br/>He lays out the facts. Gives you the time line and how things were investigated. How things happened. Precise and to the point.<br/><br/>He includes reprints of the letters that the Zodiac sent to the police and newspaper. Some of which to this day are unsolved and undecoded.<br/><br/>what is good about this boo</span>
  <span id="freeText3148949213457348115" style="display:none">What i really like about this book was how it was told and how it was layed out.<br />Mr. Graysmith was a Newspaper cartoonist who later became involved in the Zodiac case. Not by his volition but, by the Zodiacs.<br /><br />He lays out the facts. Gives you the time line and how things were investigated. How things happened. Precise and to the point.<br /><br />He includes reprints of the letters that the Zodiac sent to the police and newspaper. Some of which to this day are unsolved and undecoded.<br /><br />what is good about this book is that he does NOT let his personal emotion get to involved in the writting of this book. Yes, he was directly later involved in the case but, he does not "slant" the view of what the facts begin to lay out and where the evidance leads to.<br /><br />In the end. He does make a conclusion based upon all the facts. It is not a 100 % he did it. since this case is still unsolved and in all likleyhood will remeain that way. However, when you read the book and he lays out all the facts. Then comes to the conclusion....it is hard to deny that they had their man.<br /><br />Cool Read. Movie ws good. But, as it always is. The book is better. Read the book 1st. Then watch the movie.</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2436992601" />
    <a title="Bert Z" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/56401400-bert-z"><img alt="Bert Z" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1581827716p2/56401400.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2436992601?book_show_action=true">Jun 30, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bert Z" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bert Z" href="/user/show/56401400-bert-z">Bert Z</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2436992601" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer374932921250809998">“This is the Zodiac speaking”<br/><br/>Seriously one of the greatest true-crime books ever written. It’s up there with the likes of ‘In Cold Blood’ and ‘Helter Skelter’ in my opinion. I’ve read Zodiac countless times now and I’m always so impressed with just what a fantastic book it is. <br/><br/>True-crime authors already have a strike against them when they’re writing about a crime that’s unsolved, trying to tell a story that’s cohesive and interesting when said story is still unfinished would be a major task, on</span>
  <span id="freeText374932921250809998" style="display:none">“This is the Zodiac speaking”<br /><br />Seriously one of the greatest true-crime books ever written. It’s up there with the likes of ‘In Cold Blood’ and ‘Helter Skelter’ in my opinion. I’ve read Zodiac countless times now and I’m always so impressed with just what a fantastic book it is. <br /><br />True-crime authors already have a strike against them when they’re writing about a crime that’s unsolved, trying to tell a story that’s cohesive and interesting when said story is still unfinished would be a major task, one that few authors are able to do well, but Robert Graysmith has done a marvellous job with Zodiac.<br /><br />There are plenty of books out there about The Zodiac Killer, most of which are actually pretty good, however, the very best is this one. By all means read the others but start with this one for sure, it’ll send a shiver down your spine.<br /><br />Now for a little Jake Gyllenhaal mmmmmmmm.... :)</span>
  <a data-text-id="374932921250809998" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('38SIoInMGhPmlqFVFoAfVkqYkKkLrsGu00Pc5b3GLAkV/G+x4vO2HAMsaXcXjYnOgae4TxCwHIwY89niqO0lxA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('E2blBPaDjvXWNYEHLgjD8h4Kthyo9nMHfBswd7FNDN3ZXgIVnbwi+jOPSSUvBVVq1TWe+rPoriW3qzVwpGYFEA==')})
  }

John Wayne Gacy. Jeffrey Dahmer. The names of notorious serial killers are usually well-known; they echo in the news and in public consciousness. But most people have never heard of Israel Keyes, one of the most ambitious and terrifying serial killers in modern history. The FBI considered his behavior unprecedented. Described by a prosecutor as &quot;a force of pure evil,&quot; Keyes was a predator who struck all over the United States. He buried &quot;kill kits&quot;--cash, weapons, and body-disposal tools--in remote locations across the country. Over the course of fourteen years, Keyes would fly to a city, rent a car, and drive thousands of miles in order to use his kits. He would break into a stranger\'s house, abduct his victims in broad daylight, and kill and dispose of them in mere hours. And then he would return home to Alaska, resuming life as a quiet, reliable construction worker devoted to his only daughter.\n\nWhen journalist Maureen Callahan first heard about Israel Keyes in 2012, she was captivated by how a killer of this magnitude could go undetected by law enforcement for over a decade. And so began a project that consumed her for the next several years--uncovering the true story behind how the FBI ultimately caught Israel Keyes, and trying to understand what it means for a killer like Keyes to exist. A killer who left a path of monstrous, randomly committed crimes in his wake--many of which remain unsolved to this day.\n\nAmerican Predator is the ambitious culmination of years of interviews with key figures in law enforcement and in Keyes\'s life, and research uncovered from classified FBI files. Callahan takes us on a journey into the chilling, nightmarish mind of a relentless killer, and to the limitations of traditional law enforcement.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"5619701013117571506\" <div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer15322295968150864639">Robert Graysmith was born in Pensacola, Florida as Robert Gray Smith. He changed his name to Graysmith in 1976.<br/><br/>Graysmith is a true-crime author of the books <i><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/105760.Zodiac' title='Zodiac by Robert Graysmith' rel='nofollow noopener'>Zodiac</a>; <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/105762.Zodiac_Unmasked_The_Identity_of_America_s_Most_Elusive_Serial_Killers_Revealed' title='Zodiac Unmasked The Identity of America's Most Elusive Serial Killers Revealed by Robert Graysmith' rel='nofollow noopener'>Zodiac Unmasked: The Identity of America's Most Elusive Serial Killer</a>; <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1764313.Unabomber_A_Desire_To_Kill' title='Unabomber A Desire To Kill by Robert Graysmith' rel='nofollow noopener'>Unabomber: A Desire to Kill</a>; <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1305474.The_Sleeping_Lady_The_Trailside_Murders_Above_the_Golden_Gate' title='The Sleeping Lady The Trailside Murders Above the Golden Gate by Robert Graysmith' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Sleeping Lady: The Trailside Murders Above the Golden Gate</a>; <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1606960.Murder_Of_Bob_Crane__The_Who_Killed_the_Star_of_Hogan_s_Heroes_' title='Murder Of Bob Crane, The Who Killed the Star of Hogan's Heroes? by Robert Graysmith' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Murder of Bob Crane: Who Killed the Star of Hogan's Heroes</a>; <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/105772.The_Bell_Tower_The_Case_of_Jack_the_Ripper_Finally_Solved____in_San_Francisco' title='The Bell Tower The Case of Jack the Ripper Finally Solved... in San Francisco by Robert Graysmith' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Bel</a></i></span>
  <span id="freeText15322295968150864639" style="display:none">Robert Graysmith was born in Pensacola, Florida as Robert Gray Smith. He changed his name to Graysmith in 1976.<br /><br />Graysmith is a true-crime author of the books <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/105760.Zodiac" title="Zodiac by Robert Graysmith" rel="nofollow noopener">Zodiac</a>; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/105762.Zodiac_Unmasked_The_Identity_of_America_s_Most_Elusive_Serial_Killers_Revealed" title="Zodiac Unmasked The Identity of America's Most Elusive Serial Killers Revealed by Robert Graysmith" rel="nofollow noopener">Zodiac Unmasked: The Identity of America's Most Elusive Serial Killer</a>; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1764313.Unabomber_A_Desire_To_Kill" title="Unabomber A Desire To Kill by Robert Graysmith" rel="nofollow noopener">Unabomber: A Desire to Kill</a>; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1305474.The_Sleeping_Lady_The_Trailside_Murders_Above_the_Golden_Gate" title="The Sleeping Lady The Trailside Murders Above the Golden Gate by Robert Graysmith" rel="nofollow noopener">The Sleeping Lady: The Trailside Murders Above the Golden Gate</a>; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1606960.Murder_Of_Bob_Crane__The_Who_Killed_the_Star_of_Hogan_s_Heroes_" title="Murder Of Bob Crane, The Who Killed the Star of Hogan's Heroes? by Robert Graysmith" rel="nofollow noopener">The Murder of Bob Crane: Who Killed the Star of Hogan's Heroes</a>; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/105772.The_Bell_Tower_The_Case_of_Jack_the_Ripper_Finally_Solved____in_San_Francisco" title="The Bell Tower The Case of Jack the Ripper Finally Solved... in San Francisco by Robert Graysmith" rel="nofollow noopener">The Bell Tower: The Case of Jack the Ripper Finally Solved</a>; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2132961.Amerithrax_The_Hunt_for_the_Anthrax_Killer" title="Amerithrax The Hunt for the Anthrax Killer by Robert Graysmith" rel="nofollow noopener">Amerithrax: The Hunt for the Anthrax Killer</a>; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9529110.The_Laughing_Gorilla_The_True_Story_of_the_Hunt_for_One_of_America_s_First_Serial_Killers" title="The Laughing Gorilla The True Story of the Hunt for One of America's First Serial Killers by Robert Graysmith" rel="nofollow noopener">The Laughing Gorilla: The True Story of the Hunt for One of America's First Serial Killers</a>;</i> and <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7619031.The_Girl_in_Alfred_Hitchcock_s_Shower" title="The Girl in Alfred Hitchcock's Shower by Robert Graysmith" rel="nofollow noopener">The Girl in Alfred Hitchcock's Shower</a>
</i>.<br /><br />Graysmith's latest book <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13531820.Black_Fire_The_True_Story_of_the_Original_Tom_Sawyer__and_of_the_Mysterious_Fires_That_Baptized_Gold_Rush_Era_San_Francisco" title="Black Fire The True Story of the Original Tom Sawyer--and of the Mysterious Fires That Baptized Gold Rush-Era San Francisco by Robert Graysmith" rel="nofollow noopener">Black Fire: The True Story of the Original Tom Sawyer--and of the Mysterious Fires That Baptized Gold Rush-Era San Francisco</a>
</i> is out now. Also available as an audio book read by the author!<br /><br />Graysmith has written on the Zodiac Killer case. He first became involved in the case when he was a cartoonist for the San Francisco Chronicle. In his book <i>Serial Killers and Their Victims,</i> Graysmith blames the Zodiac murders on one-time suspect Arthur Leigh Allen. Graysmith based his book and case on actual police files.<br /><br />Two films have been based on his books: <i>Auto Focus</i> and <i>Zodiac.</i> Graysmith is portrayed in the film <i>Zodiac</i> by Jake Gyllenhaal.</span>
